FNV PBR PPLIGHTING SELECTOR DRIVER ARGUMENT PROVENANCE AUDIT

Purpose:
1. Normalize direct helper-call arguments from BDF790, the PPLighting selector/pass-entry driver.
2. Trace BDF790 resource-helper return values and stack arguments before they are forwarded into BA9EE0 helper families.
3. Keep visible PBR replacement blocked until helper params map back to concrete material fields/getters and final E7EA00 stages.
